### fetchDevices()

function fetchDevices<T>(
  target: (...args: any[]) => Promise<T>,
  _context: ClassMethodDecoratorContext<
    unknown,
    (this: unknown, ...args: any) => any
  >,
): (...args: unknown[]) => Promise<T>
